 kudarti tareeke se bina dawaaon ke ilaaj kiya jaataa he

 We were given a book of General Knowledge in our childhood days and had to memorize inventions and inventors' names from it
 sabase lambey, sabase chote or sabase lambey kaa record bhi us kitaab kaa aham hissaa hota tha

 vaise bhi is baat se to puri duniya waakif he ki itihaas banane waalon se itihaas ne puri keemat vasuuli he
 Here we are presenting for you 10 such inventors and inventors who have put everything at stake for the betterment of human civilization, even life
 1
 Max Velier - An Australian rocket pioneer with an alcohol-rocket burst on his test bench
 maiks velior germany ke rahane vaale the or vegrman rocketring socitike sadsy the
 In the year 1930, he was inventing a rocket that could accelerate automobiles
 unka yah avishkaar testing ke dauraan fat padaa or unki jaan usee samay chali gai
 2
 meri curi - applastic anemia kii vajah se marin jo beemaari unhen lambey samay tak ynikrut vikiran ke sampark main aane kii vajah se lagi
 Marie Curie is known to the world as a common inventor of radium and polonium
 ve apane hi research kiye jane vaale padaarthon or unke nikalne vaale radiation ke lambey samay tak sampark main rahane kii vajah se marin
 3
 lee si - apane dwaara hi shuru kiye gaye five pens panishment methd kii vajah se mare, lee si ne hi is sajaa kii shuruyaat kii thi
 Five Pens Punishment was an old-fashioned penalty in China
 lee si ne isaki shuruyaat tab kii thi jab vah kin vansh kaa pradhanmantri tha
 This included tattooing on someone's face, getting someone's nose cut or cutting the guilty body into four parts
 208 isa purv lee si ko thik usee prakaar dandit kiya gaya jise usne shuru kiya tha
 4
 gym fiks - america fitness revolution kaa janak daudte-daudte hi chal basajim fiks ko puri duniya ek aise insaan ke taur par jaanati he jisane jogging ko fishan statement ke taur par sthapit karne kaa kaam kiya
 Jim was just 52 years old in 1977 and one day said goodbye to the world because of a heart attack while running
 5
 Thomas Andrews - The man who designed the Titanic, who drowned with the Titanic
 thomas ireland ke rahane vaale the or ve jal sena ke ek architect the
 He also instructed not to venture into the icy waters of the Titanic and to keep a lot of lifeboats in the ship
 jabatitanic glacierase takaraayaa tab ve bacchon or mahilaon ko surakshit nikaalane kii muhim main lage the
 He was last seen crying in the deck's rooms
 unka sharir phir kabhi nahin paaya ja sakaa
 5
 elexander bogdanov - rakt ke aadan-pradaan ko nae aayam die, or tibi va malaria se peedit ek peedit ke rakt se testing ke chakkar main jaan ganvaani padi
 Bogdanov was from Russia and is known as the first person in the world to initiate the exchange of blood
 ve chirkaalik javaani hasil karne ke liye prayaas kar rahe the
 He also had some success in this direction
 haalanki jab ve ek student par research kar rahe the or khud ko rakt chadhaane kii koshish kii to malaria or tibi se peedit us student ke rogon se ve bhi peedit ho gaye or antat: jaan ganvaa baithe
 6
 maaikel dakre - ve flying taxi ko krash kar baithe jiskaa avishkaar unhone khud hi kiya tha
 Michael Dakre invented a Hawaiian taxi called the AVCEN Jetpod
 yah hawa main ud bhi saktaa tha or kshetreey ilaakon va shaharon main utar bhi saktaa tha
 In 2009, when he flew alone to test it, he accidentally lost his life
 7
 Horace Lawson Hanley - He invented the antidote submarine and went to test it with his crew
 hanle ek marine ejeeniyar va avishkaarak the jinhone pehleyudhak sabamarinaka nirmaan kiya tha
 He named it CSS Hanley
 ve saal 1863 main isaki testing ke liye pani ke bheetar gaye or apane kru ke saare saathiyon ke saath phir kabhi waapas nahin aa sake
 8
 wiliam bulak - apane hi banaae gaye printing press main pair fansaa liya, or gagarine kii vajah se jaan ganvaa baithe
 Bullock is known as the inventor of the web rotary printing press
 ve philadelphia main ek aise hi mashin ko lagava rahe the tabhi unka pair is baari mashin main funs gaya

 9
 Otto Lilianthal - invented the hand glider and lost its life when it crashed
 otto lilyenthal ko duniya glyder king ke taur par jaanati thi
 In 1896, he was flying at just 50 feet and succumbed to an accident
 ve is baat kii apeksh nahin kar rahe the lekin is dauraan lagi choton kii vajah se ve 36 maah baad nahin batch sake
 10
 francis adgaar stanley - unhen stanley steamer kaa saajha sansthaapak kaha jaataa he
 He lost his life due to collision in traffic
 francis adgaar stanley ne apane judwa bhai ke sathstanley motor kariejaki sthapana kii thi
